<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>FICO Announces Earnings of $1.82 per Share for First Quarter Fiscal 2020 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenue of $299&nbsp;million vs. $262&nbsp;million in prior year </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SAN JOSE, Calif., Jan. 30, 2020 /PRNewswire/ &#151; FICO (NYSE:FICO), a leading predictive analytics and decision management software company, today announced
results for its first fiscal quarter ended December&nbsp;31, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter Fiscal 2020 GAAP Results </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income for the quarter totaled $54.9&nbsp;million, or $1.82 per share, versus $40.0&nbsp;million, or $1.32 per share, in the prior year period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities for the quarter was $60.4&nbsp;million versus $48.9&nbsp;million in the prior year period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter Fiscal 2020 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Results </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Net Income for the quarter was $54.2&nbsp;million versus $43.9&nbsp;million in the prior year period. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> EPS for the quarter was $1.80 versus $1.45 in the prior year period. Free cash flow for the quarter was $53.9&nbsp;million versus $42.4&nbsp;million in the prior year period. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are described in the financial table captioned <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Results&#148; and are reconciled to the corresponding GAAP results in the financial
tables at the end of this release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter Fiscal 2020 GAAP Revenue </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company reported revenues of $298.5&nbsp;million for the quarter as compared to $262.3&nbsp;million reported in the prior year period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We had a great start to our fiscal 2020,&#148; said Will Lansing, chief executive officer. &#147;We achieved double-digit revenue growth, and are
delivering significant innovation throughout the organization.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Revenues for the first quarter of fiscal 2020 across each of the company&#146;s
three operating segments were as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Applications</I> revenues, which include the company&#146;s preconfigured decision management applications and
associated professional services, were $152.2&nbsp;million in the first quarter, compared to $147.7&nbsp;million in the prior year period, an increase of 3%, due primarily to increased services and SaaS subscription revenues in Originations
Solutions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Scores</I> revenues, which include the company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">business-to-business</FONT></FONT> (B2B) scoring solutions and associated professional services, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">business-to-consumer</FONT></FONT> (B2C) service, were
$115.1&nbsp;million in the first quarter, compared to $85.7&nbsp;million in the prior year period, an increase of 34%. B2B revenue increased 46% and B2C revenue increased 11% from the prior year period. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><I>Decision Management Software</I> revenues, which include Blaze Advisor<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, Xpress Optimization, Decision Management Platform and related professional services, were $31.2&nbsp;million in the first quarter compared to $28.9&nbsp;million in the prior year period, an
increase of 8%, due primarily to increased SaaS subscription and services revenues. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Outlook </B> </P>

&#147;Reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Guidance.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company to Host Conference Call </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company will host a webcast today at 5:00 p.m. Eastern Time (2:00 p.m. Pacific Time) to report its first quarter fiscal 2020 results and provide various
strategic and operational updates. The call can be accessed at FICO&#146;s web site at www.fico.com/investors. A replay of the webcast will be available at our Events Page under Past Events through January&nbsp;30, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About FICO </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FICO (NYSE: FICO) powers decisions that help
people and businesses around the world prosper. Founded in 1956 and based in Silicon Valley, the company is a pioneer in the use of predictive analytics and data science to improve operational decisions. FICO holds more than 165 US and foreign
patents on technologies that increase profitability, customer satisfaction and growth for businesses in financial services, telecommunications, health care, retail and many other industries. Using FICO solutions, businesses in more than 100
countries do everything from protecting 2.6&nbsp;billion payment cards from fraud, to helping people get credit, to ensuring that millions of airplanes and rental cars are in the right place at the right time. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Learn more at http://www.fico.com </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Join the conversation at
https://twitter.com/fico&nbsp;&amp; http://www.fico.com/en/blogs/ </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FICO is a registered trademark of Fair Isaac Corporation in the US and other countries.

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Financial Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To supplement the consolidated GAAP financial statements, the company uses the following <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures: <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> EPS, and&nbsp;free cash flow. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> net income and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
EPS exclude the impact of amortization expense, share-based compensation expense, restructuring and acquisition-related, excess tax benefit, and adjustment to tax valuation allowance items. Free cash flow excludes capital expenditures and dividends
paid.&nbsp;The presentation of these financial measures is not intended to be considered&nbsp;in isolation or as a substitute for, or superior to, the financial information prepared and presented in accordance with GAAP.</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Management uses these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures for financial and operational decision-making and as a means to
evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.&nbsp;Our&nbsp;management believes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide meaningful
supplemental information regarding our performance and liquidity by excluding certain items that may not be indicative of recurring business results including significant <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> expenses.&nbsp;We believe
management and investors benefit from referring to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in assessing our performance when planning, forecasting and analyzing future periods.&nbsp;These <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures also facilitate&nbsp;management&#146;s internal comparisons to historical performance and liquidity as well as comparisons to our competitors&#146; operating results.&nbsp;We believe
these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial&nbsp;measures are useful to investors because they allow for greater transparency with respect to key measures used by management in its financial and operating decision-making. </P>
</DIV></Center>

evaluate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT> comparisons.&nbsp;Our&nbsp;management believes these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provide meaningful
